Super Mario Bros.Super and Mega-jumps can be achieved while standing still, running or turbo running (holding down button B). Super Mario Bros.Moon gravity is a brilliant ability! It has weird and wonderful effects. Again, it works when stationary, running, or turbo running. The Moon gravity effect is more fun than Super- or Mega-jumps, but it is harder to get used to. Stay with it and you'll find that it gives the game an added twist! You can control the height of your Moon jumps. To jump really high, tap button A really quickly. To do low jumps hold down button A for about one second.
Super Mario Bros.Use this power to find new places to explore. You can even jump over the flags! (If you're playing to complete the game rather than just explore it, don't jump over the flagpoles--or else you'll get "stuck" and have to reset.)
